 What is Net Neutrality? 1
 net neutrelity ek aisi avadharana he, jisamen apeksha kii jaati he ki yujar, content, site, placeform, aplication or sanchaar ke tareekon ke aadhaar par na to bhedbhaav kiya jaae or na hi alag-alag shulk liya jaae
 2
 isamen mana ye jaataa he ki internet sarvice prowider or sarkarein net par sabhi data ko baraabar tavajjo den
